1719setTimeout(function(){link.rel="stylesheet";link.media="only x"});setTimeout(enableStylesheet,3000)};rp.poly=function(){if(rp.support()){return}

1720var links=w.document.getElementsByTagName("link");for(var i=0;i<links.length;i++){var link=links[i];if(link.rel==="preload"&&link.getAttribute("as")==="style"&&!link.getAttribute("data-loadcss")){link.setAttribute("data-loadcss",!0);rp.bindMediaToggle(link)}}};if(!rp.support()){rp.poly();var run=w.setInterval(rp.poly,500);if(w.addEventListener){w.addEventListener("load",function(){rp.poly();w.clearInterval(run)})}else if(w.attachEvent){w.attachEvent("onload",function(){rp.poly();w.clearInterval(run)})}}

1721if(typeof exports!=="undefined"){exports.loadCSS=loadCSS}

1722else{w.loadCSS=loadCSS}}(typeof global!=="undefined"?global:this))

1723</script>

2896<h1 class="cs-entry__title">

2897<span>

2898Regenerative Organic Cannabis Farming</span>

2899</h1>

2900 <div class="cs-entry__subtitle">

2901

2902 Not only is it good for the environment, but regenerative organic cannabis farming also yields densely packed nugs with rich flavors.

2903 </div>

2904

2905 </div>

2906

2907

3046 <div class="cs-entry__content-wrap">

3047

3048

3049 <div class="entry-content">

3050

3051 <p>

3052With the great state of California poised to legalize adult use cannabis in January 2018, a big debate has formed around the potential environmental impact of all that cultivation. Currently, the <a href="https://hightimes.com/news/look-fallout-californias-legalization-regulations/">

3053regulations</a>

3054 are being finalized and issues regarding everything from runoff to soil disposal have been discussed.</p>

3055

3056<p>

3057In this dialogue, sustainable farming techniques are being looked at as a potential solution to help mitigate this problem.</p>

3058

3059<p>

3060According to the Rodale Institute, “We have proven that organic agriculture and specifically, regenerative organic agriculture can sequester carbon from the atmosphere and even help to reverse climate change.”</p>

3061<div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 8px 0; clear: both;'>

3062

3063<script data-minify="1" async src="https://p2i2i5h5.rocketcdn.me/wp-content/cache/min/1/tag/js/gpt.js?ver=1634745723">

3064</script>

3071 googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

3072 googletag.enableServices();

3073 });

3074</script>

3075

3076

3077<!-- /5667049/bin0 -->

3078

3079<div id='div-gpt-ad-1582768448137-0' style='width: 300px; height: 250px; margin:0 auto'>

3080

3081 <script>

3082

3083 googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1582768448137-0'); });

3084 </script>

3085

3086</div>

3087

3088</div>

3089

3090

3091<p>

3092These regenerative farming techniques can work in cannabis gardens as well.</p>

3093

3094<p>

3095This type of agriculture could help elevate the fears that people have concerning the potential damage cannabis agriculture can leave behind. A study published in the journal, <em>

3096Environmental Research Letters, </em>

3097looked at the impact of several grow sites in Northern California and found that the sites indeed caused various <a href="https://hightimes.com/news/marijuana-farming-hurt-environment/">

3098environmental damage</a>

3099. From potentially contaminating rivers due to chemical fertilizer runoff, to increased soil erosion.</p>

3100

3101<p>

3102Regenerative farming is a type of organic farming that heals the earth while making use of it to incubate your crops.</p>

3103<div class='code-block code-block-8' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'>

3104

3105<script data-minify="1" async src="https://p2i2i5h5.rocketcdn.me/wp-content/cache/min/1/tag/js/gpt.js?ver=1634745723">

3106</script>

3107

3108<script>

3109

3110 window.googletag = window.googletag || {cmd: []};

3112 googletag.defineSlot('/5667049/blog_halfpage', [300, 250], 'div-gpt-ad-1583394553387-0').addService(googletag.pubads());

3113 googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

3114 googletag.enableServices();

3115 });

3116</script>

3117

3118

3119

3120<!-- /5667049/blog_halfpage -->

3121

3122<div id='div-gpt-ad-1583394553387-0' style="margin:0 auto">

3123

3124 <script>

3125

3126 googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1583394553387-0'); });

3127 </script>

3128

3129</div>

3130

3131

3132</div>

3133

3134

3135<p>

3136This type of farming is designed to build soil health and is comprised of practices that include cover crops, residue mulching, composting and crop rotation. These practices can also reduce climate change by restoring the biodiversity of the soil. This results in carbon drawdown and improvements in the water cycle—all of which would greatly benefit California.</p>

3137

3138<p>

3139More of these practices should be adopted when growing cannabis—as the plant heals us, so to should we attempt to &#8220;heal&#8221; the land with this plant.</p>

3140

3141<p>

3142<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-176356 pk-lazyload" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201000%20600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Regenerative Organic Cannabis Farming" width="1000" height="600" data-pk-sizes="auto" data-ls-sizes="(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px" data-pk-src="https://p2i2i5h5.rocketcdn.me/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2.jpg" data-pk-srcset="https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2.jpg 1000w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-600x360.jpg 600w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-100x60.jpg 100w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-400x240.jpg 400w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-768x461.jpg 768w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-590x354.jpg 590w" data-lazy-src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABAQMAAAAl21bKAAAAA1BMVEUAAP+KeNJXAAAAAXRSTlMAQObYZgAAAAlwSFlzAAAOxAAADsQBlSsOGwAAAApJREFUCNdjYAAAAAIAAeIhvDMAAAAASUVORK5CYII=" >

3143<noscript>

3144<img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-176356 pk-lazyload" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABAQMAAAAl21bKAAAAA1BMVEUAAP+KeNJXAAAAAXRSTlMAQObYZgAAAAlwSFlzAAAOxAAADsQBlSsOGwAAAApJREFUCNdjYAAAAAIAAeIhvDMAAAAASUVORK5CYII=" alt="Regenerative Organic Cannabis Farming" width="1000" height="600" data-pk-sizes="auto" data-ls-sizes="(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px" data-pk-src="https://p2i2i5h5.rocketcdn.me/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2.jpg" data-pk-srcset="https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2.jpg 1000w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-600x360.jpg 600w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-100x60.jpg 100w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-400x240.jpg 400w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-768x461.jpg 768w, https://3ncb884ou5e49t9eb3fpeur1-wpengine.netdna-ssl.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/12/Regenerative-Organic-Cannabis-Farming-2-590x354.jpg 590w" >

3145</noscript>

3146</p>

3147<div class='code-block code-block-6' style='margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'>

3148

3149<script data-minify="1" async src="https://p2i2i5h5.rocketcdn.me/wp-content/cache/min/1/tag/js/gpt.js?ver=1634745723">

3150</script>

3171

3172</div>

3173</div>

3174

3175

3176<p>

3177As more and more people cultivate the plant, the risks to the environment grow.</p>

3178

3179<p>

3180Not all of these new farmers will practice <a href="https://hightimes.com/grow/organics-for-beginners/">

3181organic or sustainable agriculture</a>

3182. According to a study from the Center on Food Security and the Environment, over the last five years, there has been a 50 to 100 percent increase in land being used to cultivate cannabis. From water use to land erosion to chemical nutrients being used, the environmental impact is huge.</p>

3183

3184<p>

3185This is why practices like regenerative farming will be so important under the new regulatory landscape.</p>

3186

3187<p>

3188As the new regulations sweep into effect January 2018, a lot of California’s growers will have to make drastic changes to their cultivation techniques; hopefully, most will choose a path leading towards sustainability.</p>

3189

3190<p>

3191In an age of mainstream cannabis, it is crucial that we act as shining examples in all aspects of the industry, including the environmental impact we, as cannabis growers, leave behind.</p>

3192

3193<p>

3194Not only that but these techniques often also improve flavor and bud structure—returning densely packed nugs that have deep rich flavors as a result of the terroir. Much like grapes, the flavor of cannabis is also affected by the environment. This is why the same strain grown by different growers under different conditions will vary so much. Over time, we will come to see that where your cannabis is grown, as well as how it&#8217;s grown, will be a deciding factor for the discerning cannabis consumer.</p>

3195
